    "#### Apply ADI"

   "source": [
    "This uses a Principal Components Analysis approach to clean up the cubes."
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": false
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "\n",
    "# this is our ADI function\n",
    "from ADI import apply_ADI\n",
    "outim = apply_ADI(filenames,     # List of filenames containing the aligned cubes and their variane\n",
    "                    minsep=10,   # Radial separations at which to suppress weights\n",
    "                    maxsep=70,   # in low-rank approximation to the PSF\n",
    "                    nvec=10,     # Number of principal components to fit at each wavelength\n",
    "                    ivar=True)   # whether we use the inverse variance weights or not\n",
    "\n",
    "# export the new cube which has been cleaned by ADI\n",
    "hdr = fits.open(new_cubenames[0])[0].header # this is just so we have a header to attach to the data\n",
    "out = fits.HDUList(fits.PrimaryHDU(outim,hdr))\n",
    "out.writeto(charisfolder+'ADI_recen.fits',clobber=True)"
   ]
